# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with:

**18 Key Files** implementing the state machine:
- State definition files (ClassicGroupState, ConsumerGroupState, StreamsGroupState, ShareGroupState)
- Group implementation classes (ClassicGroup, ConsumerGroup, StreamsGroup, ShareGroup)
- Member classes and assignment builders
- Core coordinator classes (GroupMetadataManager, GroupCoordinatorShard, GroupCoordinatorService)

**25+ Key Symbols** including:
- State enums and group classes
- Transition methods (`transitionTo`, `assertValidTransition`)
- Request handlers (`classicGroupJoin`, `classicGroupSync`, `classicGroupHeartbeat`)
- Service methods (`joinGroup`, `syncGroup`)

**State Machine Architecture:**

1. **Classic Groups** - Five states: EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE → DEAD
   - Join phase: transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE
   - Sync phase: transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE then STABLE
   - Rebalance: triggered by membership changes via heartbeat

2. **Modern Consumer/Streams/Share Groups** - Alternative state machines with similar lifecycle patterns

3. **Call Chain** - Shows the flow from public API (GroupCoordinator interface) → service → shard → metadata manager → group state transitions

The implementation uses a record-based approach where all state transitions generate CoordinatorRecords for persistence and recovery.

`ClassicGroup.transitionTo(COMPLETING_REBALANCE)` then `transitionTo(STABLE)`\\n\\n3. **Rebalance** (triggered by membership changes): Detected through heartbeats (`classicGroupHeartbeat`) and member timeouts, causing transition back to PREPARING_REBALANCE.\\n\\n## Key Implementation Files\\n\\n**State Definitions**:\\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java` -   "text": "The Apache Kafka consumer group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java files in the group-coordinator module. The state machine handles three main group types: Classic Groups, Consumer Groups (modern protocol), and Streams Groups.\n\n## State Definitions\n\n**Classic Groups** (legacy protocol): The state machine is defined in `ClassicGroupState.java` and includes five states:\n- EMPTY: Group has no members\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group is preparing to rebalance (Join phase)\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group awaits state assignment from leader (Sync phase)\n- STABLE: Group is stable\n- DEAD: Group is being removed\n\nTransitions are validated through the `validPreviousStates()` method in `ClassicGroupState.java`, which enforces state machine rules like: EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE.\n\n**Modern Consumer Groups**: Defined in `ConsumerGroup.java` with states:\n- EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\n\nMember-level states are in `MemberState.java`:\n- STABLE: Member is reconciled with target assignment\n- UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS: Member must revoke partitions\n- UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS: Member waits for partitions to be released\n\n**Streams Groups**: Defined in `StreamsGroup.java` with states:\n- EMPTY, NOT_READY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\n\n**Share Groups**: Defined in `ShareGroup.java` with states:\n- EMPTY, STABLE, DEAD\n\n## State Transition Logic\n\nThe primary state transitions occur through three main API calls:\n\n1. **Join Phase** (`classicGroupJoin` in `GroupMetadataManager.java`): Members join the group, triggering transition to PREPARING_REBALANCE state. Handled by:\n   - `GroupCoordinator.joinGroup()` interface\n   - `GroupCoordinatorService.joinGroup()` implementation\n   - `GroupCoordinatorShard.classicGroupJoin()` routing\n   - `GroupMetadataManager.classicGroupJoin()` logic\n   - `ClassicGroup.transitionTo(PREPARING_REBALANCE)`\n\n2. **Sync Phase** (`classicGroupSync` in `GroupMetadataManager.java`): Leader provides assignment, triggering transition to COMPLETING_REBALANCE then STABLE. Handled by:\n   - `GroupCoordinator.syncGroup()` interface\n   - `GroupCoordinatorService.syncGroup()` implementation\n   - `GroupCoordinatorShard.classicGroupSync()` routing\n   - `GroupMetadataManager.classicGroupSync()` logic\n   - `ClassicGroup.transitionTo(COMPLETING_REBALANCE)` then `transitionTo(STABLE)`\n\n3. **Rebalance** (triggered by membership changes): Detected through heartbeats (`classicGroupHeartbeat`) and member timeouts, causing transition back to PREPARING_REBALANCE.\n\n## Key Implementation Files\n\n**State Definitions**:\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java` - Classic group states and valid transitions\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java` - Modern consumer group states\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java` - Member-level states\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java` - Streams group states\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java` - Share group states\n\n**Transition Orchestration**:\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java` - Implements `transitionTo()` and `assertValidTransition()` methods\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java` - Core orchestrator with `classicGroupJoin()`, `classicGroupSync()`, `classicGroupHeartbeat()`\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java` - Shard-level coordinator routing requests\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java` - Service-level implementation\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java` - Public interface definition\n\n**Assignment Builders** (for state machine reconciliation):\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java` - Reconciles member state with target assignment for consumer groups\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java` - Reconciles member state for streams groups\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java` - Reconciles member state for share groups\n\nThe state machine ensures consistency through record-based updates, with all transitions generating CoordinatorRecords that are persisted and replayed for recovery."
